{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01N3PAGgsJ5Yqpmem9tPjYBV","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Good! Now I understand the structure better. The IWL_PCI_DEVICE macro is defined on lines 78-81, and the iwl_hw_card_ids array is the PCI device ID table.\n\nHowever, looking at the code structure:\n1. There's the IWL_PCI_DEVICE table (iwl_hw_card_ids) which is used for initial PCI device matching\n2. There's the IWL_DEV_INFO table which is used for more specific device info lookupThe bug is about \"missing PCI subdevice entries\" - which most likely refers to missing entries in one or both of
